## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |

| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# TiDB SQL Privilege Check and RBAC Enforcement Audit

## Your Task

Audit the privilege and RBAC enforcement in pingcap/tidb. Find all Go source files under pkg/privilege/ and pkg/planner/ that implement privilege checking for SQL statements. Identify: the PrivilegeManager interface, the MySQLPrivilege cache, the RequestVerification method and its callers, the role graph resolution logic, and any files that map SQL statement types to required privileges. For each file report the path and its role in the privilege check flow.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/tidb--v8.5.0.

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

56-assistanttext-
I've completed a comprehensive audit of the privilege and RBAC enforcement system in TiDB. The analysis is saved in `/workspace/answer.json` with the following key findings:

## Summary

The privilege enforcement system in TiDB consists of **9 critical files** organized into layers:

### Core Components:

1. **Manager Interface** (`pkg/privilege/privilege.go`) - Defines the privilege management contract with methods for checking static and dynamic privileges

2. **MySQLPrivilege Cache** (`pkg/privilege/privileges/cache.go`) - In-memory cache with:
   - Role graph resolution using BFS (`FindAllRole()` method)
   - Four-level privilege checking: global → database → table → column
   - `LoadRoleGraph()` for loading mysql.role_edges table
   - Direct role graph edge detection via `FindRole()`

3. **UserPrivileges** (`pkg/privilege/privileges/privileges.go`) - Session-level wrapper that delegates to MySQLPrivilege with support for dynamic privileges and auth plugins

4. **VisitInfo System** (`pkg/planner/core/planbuilder.go`) - Struct that maps SQL statements to required privileges

5. **Privilege Mapping** (`pkg/planner/core/logical_plan_builder.go`) - Functions that populate visitInfo for different statement types (SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE, CREATE, ALTER, GRANT, etc.)

6. **Privilege Validation** (`pkg/planner/core/optimizer.go`) - `CheckPrivilege()` and `VisitInfo4PrivCheck()` functions that validate all collected privileges

7. **Planning Integration** (`pkg/planner/optimize.go`) - Entry point in the optimization pipeline

8. **Plan Cache** (`pkg/planner/core/plan_cache.go`) - Re-validation of privileges for cached plans

9. **Auth Connection** (`pkg/privilege/conn/conn.go`) - Interface for pluggable authentication mechanisms

The complete flow document shows how r

Architecture\\n\\nThe privilege and RBAC enforcement system in TiDB is a multi-layered architecture with privilege checking occurring at both planning and execution stages:\\n\\n### 1. Core Manager Interface (pkg/privilege/privilege.go)\\n\\n**Manager Interface** (lines 44-123):\\n- Central abstraction for privilege operations\\n- Key methods:\\n  - `RequestVerification(activeRole, db, table, column, priv)`: Checks user privilege at global, database, table, or column level\\n  - `RequestDynamicVerification(activeRoles, privName, grantable)`: Checks dynamic privileges (BACKUP_ADMIN, RESTORE_ADMIN, SYSTEM_USER, etc.)\\n  - `RequestVerificationWithUser()`: Verifies specific user privilege\\n  - `ConnectionVerification()`: Verifies privilege during connection establishment\\n  - `ActiveRoles()`, `GetAllRoles()`, `GetDefaultRoles()`: Role management\\n  - `FindEdge()`: Checks role graph edges\\n\\n**Context Binding Functions**:\\n- `BindPrivilegeManager()`: Attaches Manager to session context (lines 127-129)\\n- `GetPrivilegeManager()`: Retrieves Manager from context (lines 137-143)\\n\\n### 2. MySQLPrivilege Cache (pkg/privilege/privileges/cache.go)\\n\\n**MySQLPrivilege struct** (lines 286-300):\\nThe in-memory privilege cache implementing the core privilege lookup logic:\\n- Embedded `immutable` struct containing: user records, db records, tables_priv records, columns_priv records, default_roles, global_priv, dynamic privileges, and role graph\\n- Extended struct for accelerated lookups via maps\\n\\n**Role Graph Resolution** (lines 314-348):\\n- `FindAllRole()` (lines 314-337): Breadth-first search (BFS) algorithm to traverse role hierarchy and find all effective roles for a user\\n  - Uses queue-based iteration over roleGraph to discover transitive role memberships\\n  - Maintains visited set to prevent cycles\\n  - Critical for determining which privileges a user has through role inheritance\\n\\n- `FindRole()` (lines 339-348): Detects direct edges between users and roles\\n\\n- `roleGraphEdgesTable` (lines 248-264): Represents relationships between users/roles\\n  - `Find(user, host)`: Checks if a specific role is in the graph\\n\\n- `LoadRoleGraph()` (lines 540-548): Loads mysql.role_edges table from database into memory cache\\n  - Initializes the roleGraph map structure\\n  - Uses `decodeRoleEdgesTable()` to parse SQL results\\n\\n**RequestVerification Implementation** (lines 1332-1387):\\nCore privilege checking logic with four-level scope checking:\\n1. **Global level**: Checks user privileges (lines 1342-1350)\\n2. **Database level**: Checks DB-scoped privileges (lines 1352-1360)\\n3. **Table level**: Checks table and column privileges (lines 1362-1373)\\n4. **Column level**: Checks column-specific privileges (lines 1375-1384)\\n\\nFor each scope, the implementation:\\n- Iterates through all effective roles via `FindAllUserEffectiveRoles()`\\n- Accumulates privileges with bitwise OR\\n- Returns true if the required privilege is present at any scope level\\n\\n**Helper Methods**:\\n- `FindAllUserEffectiveRoles()` (lines 302-312): Filters active roles to only those actually granted to the user\\n- `LoadUserTable()`, `LoadDBTable()`, `LoadTablesPrivTable()`, `LoadColumnsPrivTable()`: Load privilege tables\\n\\n### 3. UserPrivileges Wrapper (pkg/privilege/privileges/privileges.go)\\n\\n**UserPrivileges struct** (lines 74-85):\\nImplements `privilege.Manager` interface, serving as a wrapper around MySQLPrivilege:\\n- Stores user identity (username, hostname)\\n- Maintains reference to MySQLPrivilege Handle (underlying cache)\\n- Integrates extension system hooks for auth plugins\\n\\n**Key Methods**:\\n- `RequestVerification()` (lines 141-150): Delegates to MySQLPrivilege.RequestVerification() with user identity\\n- `RequestDynamicVerification()` (lines 125-139): Handles dynamic privilege checks with fallback to SUPER privilege\\n- `NewUserPrivileges()` (lines 87-94): Factory for creating UserPrivileges instances\\n\\n**Dynamic Privileges** (lines 53-70):\\nRegistered dynamic privileges include:\\n- BACKUP_ADMIN, RESTORE_ADMIN, SYSTEM_USER, SYSTEM_VARIABLES_ADMIN\\n- ROLE_ADMIN, CONNECTION_ADMIN, PLACEMENT_ADMIN\\n- RESTRICTED_* variants (TABLES_ADMIN, VARIABLES_ADMIN, etc.)\\n- RESOURCE_GROUP_ADMIN, RESOURCE_GROUP_USER\\n\\n### 4. SQL Statement Privilege Mapping (pkg/planner/core/)\\n\\n**visitInfo struct** (planbuilder.go, lines 81-92):\\nRepresents a privilege requirement for SQL statement execution:\\n```go\\ntype visitInfo struct {\\n    privilege       mysql.PrivilegeType  // Static privilege required\\n    db              string               // Database scope\\n    table           string               // Table scope\\n    column          string               // Column scope\\n    dynamicPrivs    []string             // Dynamic privileges (alternatives)\\n    dynamicWithGrant bool                // Whether GRANT option required\\n}\\n```\\n\\n**Statement-to-Privilege Mappings** (logical_plan_builder.go):\\n\\nDifferent SQL statements add visitInfo entries during planning:\\n- **SELECT statements**: Adds SelectPriv (line 3471)\\n- **INSERT statements** (buildInsert, line 4396): Adds InsertPriv; adds DeletePriv if ON DUPLICATE KEY REPLACE\\n- **UPDATE statements**: Adds UpdatePriv and SelectPriv\\n- **DELETE statements**: Adds DeletePriv and SelectPriv\\n- **CREATE TABLE**: Adds CreatePriv (special handling for temporary tables with CreateTMPTablePriv)\\n- **ALTER TABLE**: Adds AlterPriv and SelectPriv\\n- **CREATE/DROP/ALTER DATABASE**: Adds CreatePriv/DropPriv\\n- **GRANT/REVOKE**: Adds GrantPriv or dynamic privilege checks\\n- **CREATE/DROP USER**: Adds CreateUserPriv or CreateRolePriv\\n- **ADMIN statements**: Various ADMIN privileges based on operation type\\n\\n**Helper Functions**:\\n- `appendVisitInfo()` (logical_plan_builder.go, lines 7105-7109): Appends static privilege requirement\\n- `appendDynamicVisitInfo()` (logical_plan_builder.go, lines 7096-7100): Appends dynamic privilege requirement\\n- `appendVisitInfoIsRestrictedUser()` (planbuilder.go, lines 3737-3750): Adds RESTRICTED_USER_ADMIN check when SEM is enabled\\n\\n### 5. Privilege Checking Pipeline (pkg/planner/core/optimizer.go)\\n\\n**CheckPrivilege()** (lines 125-150):\\nValidates accumulated visitInfo entries:\\n1. Iterates through all visitInfo entries collected during planning\\n2. For each entry:\\n   - If dynamic privilege (mysql.ExtendedPriv):\\n     - Calls `RequestDynamicVerification()` for each privilege name\\n     - Requires at least one privilege match (OR logic)\\n   - If static privilege:\\n     - Calls `RequestVerification()` with db/table/column scope\\n     - Requires exact privilege match\\n3. Returns error if any privilege check fails\\n\\n**VisitInfo4PrivCheck()** (lines 152-207):\\nPost-processing of visitInfo for temporary table handling:\\n- For CREATE TEMPORARY TABLE: Changes CreatePriv to CreateTMPTablePriv at database scope\\n- For other operations on local temporary tables: Filters out unnecessary privilege checks\\n- Ensures compliance with MySQL temporary table privilege semantics\\n\\n### 6. Planning-Time Privilege Checking (pkg/planner/optimize.go)\\n\\nPrivilege checking integration point during statement optimization:\\n- **HandleOptimize()** (lines 495-510): After logical plan building, collects visitInfo\\n- Calls `core.VisitInfo4PrivCheck()` to adjust for temporary tables\\n- Invokes `core.CheckPrivilege()` to validate all collected requirements\\n- Blocks execution if privileges insufficient\\n\\n### 7. Authentication Connection (pkg/privilege/conn/conn.go)\\n\\n**AuthConn interface** (lines 19-30):\\nEnables auth plugins to interact with client during authentication:\\n- `WriteAuthMoreData()`: Send authentication challenge data\\n- `ReadPacket()`: Receive authentication response from client\\n- `Flush()`: Transmit buffered data to client\\n\\nSupports pluggable authentication mechanisms (PAM, LDAP, JWT, etc.)\\n\\n### 8. Privilege Check Flow Summary\\n\\nEnd-to-end flow:\\n```\\nSQL Statement\\n    \u2193\\nLogical Plan Builder (logical_plan_builder.go)\\n  - Collects visitInfo for each table/operation\\n  - appendVisitInfo() for static privileges\\n  - appendDynamicVisitInfo() for dynamic privileges\\n    \u2193\\nOptimizer (optimizer.go)\\n  - VisitInfo4PrivCheck() adjusts for temp tables\\n  - CheckPrivilege() validates all visitInfo\\n    \u2193\\nCheckPrivilege() (optimizer.go, line 126-150)\\n  - For each visitInfo:\\n    - Dynamic: RequestDynamicVerification()\\n    - Static: RequestVerification()\\n    \u2193\\nUserPrivileges.RequestVerification() (privileges.go, line 142)\\n  - Delegates to MySQLPrivilege via Handle.Get()\\n    \u2193\\nMySQLPrivilege.RequestVerification() (cache.go, line 1332)\\n  - Calls FindAllUserEffectiveRoles()\\n  - Checks global/db/table/column privilege levels\\n  - Iterates through role graph for inherited privileges\\n    \u2193\\nFindAllRole() (cache.go, line 314) - BFS Role Resolution\\n  - Traverses roleGraph via breadth-first search\\n  - Returns all effective roles including inherited ones\\n```\\n\\n### 9. Role Inheritance and Dynamic Privilege Support\\n\\n**Role Graph Handling**:\\n- `roleGraph` map keyed by \\\"user@host\\\" \\n- Each entry contains map of granted roles\\n- Supports recursive role inheritance via BFS traversal\\n- Critical for supporting ROLE_ADMIN operations and role-based privilege granularity\\n\\n**Dynamic Privilege Fallback**:\\n- SUPER privilege grants all dynamic privileges (except when SEM enabled)\\n- Extension plugins can provide additional authorization logic\\n- Support for explicit dynamic privilege grants without SUPER\\n\\n### Key Files in Privilege Check Flow:\\n\\n1. **pkg/privilege/privilege.go**: Manager interface definition and context binding\\n2. **pkg/privilege/privileges/cache.go**: In-memory privilege cache with role graph resolution\\n3. **pkg/privilege/privileges/privileges.go**: UserPrivileges wrapper for current session\\n4. **pkg/planner/core/planbuilder.go**: visitInfo struct and plan builder initialization\\n5. **pkg/planner/core/logical_plan_builder.go**: Statement-specific visitInfo population\\n6. **pkg/planner/core/optimizer.go**: Central privilege checking and temporary table handling\\n7. **pkg/planner/optimize.go**: Planning pipeline integration point\\n8. **pkg/planner/core/plan_cache.go**: Privilege re-verification for cached plans\\n9. **pkg/privilege/conn/conn.go**: Authentication connection interface for plugins\\n\\nThis architecture ensures comprehensive RBAC enforcement where every SQL statement is validated against the user's direct privileges and role-inherited privileges before execution.\\n\"\n}\n",

Architecture\\n\\nThe privilege and RBAC enforcement system in TiDB is a multi-layered architecture with privilege checking occurring at both planning and execution stages:\\n\\n### 1. Core Manager Interface (pkg/privilege/privilege.go)\\n\\n**Manager Interface** (lines 44-123):\\n- Central abstraction for privilege operations\\n- Key methods:\\n  - `RequestVerification(activeRole, db, table, column, priv)`: Checks user privilege at global, database, table, or column level\\n  - `RequestDynamicVerification(activeRoles, privName, grantable)`: Checks dynamic privileges (BACKUP_ADMIN, RESTORE_ADMIN, SYSTEM_USER, etc.)\\n  - `RequestVerificationWithUser()`: Verifies specific user privilege\\n  - `ConnectionVerification()`: Verifies privilege during connection establishment\\n  - `ActiveRoles()`, `GetAllRoles()`, `GetDefaultRoles()`: Role management\\n  - `FindEdge()`: Checks role graph edges\\n\\n**Context Binding Functions**:\\n- `BindPrivilegeManager()`: Attaches Manager to session context (lines 127-129)\\n- `GetPrivilegeManager()`: Retrieves Manager from context (lines 137-143)\\n\\n### 2. MySQLPrivilege Cache (pkg/privilege/privileges/cache.go)\\n\\n**MySQLPrivilege struct** (lines 286-300):\\nThe in-memory privilege cache implementing the core privilege lookup logic:\\n- Embedded `immutable` struct containing: user records, db records, tables_priv records, columns_priv records, default_roles, global_priv, dynamic privileges, and role graph\\n- Extended struct for accelerated lookups via maps\\n\\n**Role Graph Resolution** (lines 314-348):\\n- `FindAllRole()` (lines 314-337): Breadth-first search (BFS) algorithm to traverse role hierarchy and find all effective roles for a user\\n  - Uses queue-based iteration over roleGraph to discover transitive role memberships\\n  - Maintains visited set to prevent cycles\\n  - Critical for determining which privileges a user has through role inheritance\\n\\n- `FindRole()` (lines 339-348): Detects direct edges between users and roles\\n\\n- `roleGraphEdgesTable` (lines 248-264): Represents relationships between users/roles\\n  - `Find(user, host)`: Checks if a specific role is in the graph\\n\\n- `LoadRoleGraph()` (lines 540-548): Loads mysql.role_edges table from database into memory cache\\n  - Initializes the roleGraph map structure\\n  - Uses `decodeRoleEdgesTable()` to parse SQL results\\n\\n**RequestVerification Implementation** (lines 1332-1387):\\nCore privilege checking logic with four-level scope checking:\\n1. **Global level**: Checks user privileges (lines 1342-1350)\\n2. **Database level**: Checks DB-scoped privileges (lines 1352-1360)\\n3. **Table level**: Checks table and column privileges (lines 1362-1373)\\n4. **Column level**: Checks column-specific privileges (lines 1375-1384)\\n\\nFor each scope, the implementation:\\n- Iterates through all effective roles via `FindAllUserEffectiveRoles()`\\n- Accumulates privileges with bitwise OR\\n- Returns true if the required privilege is present at any scope level\\n\\n**Helper Methods**:\\n- `FindAllUserEffectiveRoles()` (lines 302-312): Filters active roles to only those actually granted to the user\\n- `LoadUserTable()`, `LoadDBTable()`, `LoadTablesPrivTable()`, `LoadColumnsPrivTable()`: Load privilege tables\\n\\n### 3. SQL Statement Privilege Mapping (pkg/planner/core/)\\n\\n**visitInfo struct** (planbuilder.go, lines 81-92):\\nRepresents a privilege requirement for SQL statement execution:\\n```go\\ntype visitInfo struct {\\n    privilege       mysql.PrivilegeType  // Static privilege required\\n    db              string               // Database scope\\n    table           string               // Table scope\\n    column          string               // Column scope\\n    dynamicPrivs    []string             // Dynamic privileges (alternatives)\\n    dynamicWithGrant bool                // Whether GRANT option required\\n}\\n```\\n\\n**Statement-to-Privilege Mappings** (logical_plan_builder.go):\\n\\nDifferent SQL statements add visitInfo entries during planning:\\n- **SELECT statements**: Adds SelectPriv (line 3471)\\n- **INSERT statements** (buildInsert, line 4396): Adds InsertPriv; adds DeletePriv if ON DUPLICATE KEY REPLACE\\n- **UPDATE statements**: Adds UpdatePriv and SelectPriv\\n- **DELETE statements**: Adds DeletePriv and SelectPriv\\n- **CREATE TABLE**: Adds CreatePriv (special handling for temporary tables with CreateTMPTablePriv)\\n- **ALTER TABLE**: Adds AlterPriv and SelectPriv\\n- **CREATE/DROP/ALTER DATABASE**: Adds CreatePriv/DropPriv\\n- **GRANT/REVOKE**: Adds GrantPriv or dynamic privilege checks\\n- **CREATE/DROP USER**: Adds CreateUserPriv or CreateRolePriv\\n- **ADMIN statements**: Various ADMIN privileges based on operation type\\n\\n**Helper Functions**:\\n- `appendVisitInfo()` (logical_plan_builder.go, lines 7105-7109): Appends static privilege requirement\\n- `appendDynamicVisitInfo()` (logical_plan_builder.go, lines 7096-7100): Appends dynamic privilege requirement\\n- `appendVisitInfoIsRestrictedUser()` (planbuilder.go, lines 3737-3750): Adds RESTRICTED_USER_ADMIN check when SEM is enabled\\n\\n### 5. Privilege Checking Pipeline (pkg/planner/core/optimizer.go)\\n\\n**CheckPrivilege()** (lines 125-150):\\nValidates accumulated visitInfo entries:\\n1. Iterates through all visitInfo entries collected during planning\\n2. For each entry:\\n   - If dynamic privilege (mysql.ExtendedPriv):\\n     - Calls `RequestDynamicVerification()` for each privilege name\\n     - Requires at least one privilege match (OR logic)\\n   - If static privilege:\\n     - Calls `RequestVerification()` with db/table/column scope\\n     - Requires exact privilege match\\n3. Returns error if any privilege check fails\\n\\n**VisitInfo4PrivCheck()** (lines 152-207):\\nPost-processing of visitInfo for temporary table handling:\\n- For CREATE TEMPORARY TABLE: Changes CreatePriv to CreateTMPTablePriv at database scope\\n- For other operations on local temporary tables: Filters out unnecessary privilege checks\\n- Ensures compliance with MySQL temporary table privilege semantics\\n\\n### 6. Planning-Time Privilege Checking (pkg/planner/optimize.go)\\n\\nPrivilege checking integration point during statement optimization:\\n- **HandleOptimize()** (lines 495-510): After logical plan building, collects visitInfo\\n- Calls `core.VisitInfo4PrivCheck()` to adjust for temporary tables\\n- Invokes `core.CheckPrivilege()` to validate all collected requirements\\n- Blocks execution if privileges insufficient\\n\\n### 7. Authentication Connection (pkg/privilege/conn/conn.go)\\n\\n**AuthConn interface** (lines 19-30):\\nEnables auth plugins to interact with client during authentication:\\n- `WriteAuthMoreData()`: Send authentication challenge data\\n- `ReadPacket()`: Receive authentication response from client\\n- `Flush()`: Transmit buffered data to client\\n\\nSupports pluggable authentication mechanisms (PAM, LDAP, JWT, etc.)\\n\\n### 8. Privilege Check Flow Summary\\n\\nEnd-to-end flow:\\n```\\nSQL Statement\\n    \u2193\\nLogical Plan Builder (logical_plan_builder.go)\\n  - Collects visitInfo for each table/operation\\n  - appendVisitInfo() for static privileges\\n  - appendDynamicVisitInfo() for dynamic privileges\\n    \u2193\\nOptimizer (optimizer.go)\\n  - VisitInfo4PrivCheck() adjusts for temp tables\\n  - CheckPrivilege() validates all visitInfo\\n    \u2193\\nCheckPrivilege() (optimizer.go, line 126-150)\\n  - For each visitInfo:\\n    - Dynamic: RequestDynamicVerification()\\n    - Static: RequestVerification()\\n    \u2193\\nUserPrivileges.RequestVerification() (privileges.go, line 142)\\n  - Delegates to MySQLPrivilege via Handle.Get()\\n    \u2193\\nMySQLPrivilege.RequestVerification() (cache.go, line 1332)\\n  - Calls FindAllUserEffectiveRoles()\\n  - Checks global/db/table/column privilege levels\\n  - Iterates through role graph for inherited privileges\\n    \u2193\\nFindAllRole() (cache.go, line 314) - BFS Role Resolution\\n  - Traverses roleGraph via breadth-first search\\n  - Returns all effective roles including inherited ones\\n```\\n\\n### 9. Role Inheritance and Dynamic Privilege Support\\n\\n**Role Graph Handling**:\\n- `roleGraph` map keyed by \\\"user@host\\\" \\n- Each entry contains map of granted roles\\n- Supports recursive role inheritance via BFS traversal\\n- Critical for supporting ROLE_ADMIN operations and role-based privilege granularity\\n\\n**Dynamic Privilege Fallback**:\\n- SUPER privilege grants all dynamic privileges (except when SEM enabled)\\n- Extension plugins can provide additional authorization logic\\n- Support for explicit dynamic privilege grants without SUPER\\n\\n### Key Files in Privilege Check Flow:\\n\\n1. **pkg/privilege/privilege.go**: Manager interface definition and context binding\\n2. **pkg/privilege/privileges/cache.go**: In-memory privilege cache with role graph resolution\\n3. **pkg/privilege/privileges/privileges.go**: UserPrivileges wrapper for current session\\n4. **pkg/planner/core/planbuilder.go**: visitInfo struct and plan builder initialization\\n5. **pkg/planner/core/logical_plan_builder.go**: Statement-specific visitInfo population\\n6. **pkg/planner/core/optimizer.go**: Central privilege checking and temporary table handling\\n7. **pkg/planner/optimize.go**: Planning pipeline integration point\\n8. **pkg/planner/core/plan_cache.go**: Privilege re-verification for cached plans\\n9. **pkg/privilege/conn/conn.go**: Authentication connection interface for plugins\\n\\nThis architecture ensures comprehensive RBAC enforcement where every SQL statement is validated against the user's direct privileges and role-inherited privileges before execution.\\n\"\n}\n",
